,DECODE(TAI.UNYO, '0', '0:–¢ŠJ’Ê', '1', '1:‰^—p’†', '2', '2:‹xŽ~’†', TAI.UNYO) AS UNYO     ,TAI.TAITNM     ,TAI.SDNM     ,DECODE(TAI.NCU_SET, '3', '3:–³', TAI.NCU_SET||':—L') AS NCU_SETNM2     ,TAI.TIZUNO     ,TAI.METASYU     ,TAI.SIJI_BIKO1     ,TAI.SYONO     ,TAI.STD_KYOTEN     ,TAI.AITNM     ,TAI.SDTBIK1     ,TAI.FKINM     ,TAI.TSADNM     ,TAI.TKIGNM     ,TAI.JAKENREN     ,TAI.RENTIME     ,TAI.SDSKBN_NAI     ,(CASE         WHEN TAI.METFUKKI = '1' THEN '1:ƒ[ƒ^•œ‹A'         WHEN TAI.HOAN = '1' THEN '1:•ÛˆÀ'         WHEN TAI.GASGIRE = '1' THEN '1:ƒKƒXØ‚ê'         WHEN TAI.KIGKOSYO = '1' THEN '1:Ší‹ïŒÌá'         WHEN TAI.CSNTGEN = '1' THEN '1:‚»‚Ì‘¼'         ELSE NULL      END) AS GAS_FLG     ,TAI.SHUGOU || DECODE(PL6.NAME,NULL,NULL,':'||PL6.NAME) AS SHUGOU     ,DECODE(TAI.GASMUMU, '0', '0:—L', TAI.GASMUMU||':–³') AS GASMUMU     ,DECODE(TAI.ORGENIN, '1', '1:ƒKƒXŠí‹ï', TAI.ORGENIN) AS ORGENIN     ,DECODE(TAI.GASGUMU, '0', '0:—L', TAI.GASGUMU||':–³') AS GASGUMU     ,DECODE(TAI.METYOINA, '0', '0:—Ç', TAI.METYOINA||':”Û') AS METYOINA     ,DECODE(TAI.HOSKOKAN, '0', '0:ŽÀŽ{', TAI.HOSKOKAN||':–¢ŽÀŽ{') AS HOSKOKAN     ,DECODE(TAI.TYOUYOINA, '0', '0:—Ç', TAI.TYOUYOINA||':”Û') AS TYOUYOINA     ,DECODE(TAI.VALYOINA, '0', '0:—Ç', TAI.VALYOINA||':”Û') AS VALYOINA     ,DECODE(TAI.COYOINA, '0', '0:—Ç', TAI.COYOINA||':”Û') AS COYOINA     ,DECODE(TAI.KYUHAIUMU, '0', '0:—Ç', TAI.KYUHAIUMU||':”Û') AS KYUHAIUMU     ,DECODE(TAI.KIGTAIYO, '1', '1:—L', TAI.KIGTAIYO||':–³') AS KIGTAIYO FROM     D20_TAIOU TAI    LEFT JOIN SHAMAS KOK ON TAI.KURACD = KOK.CLI_CD                           AND TAI.ACBCD = KOK.HAN_CD                          AND TAI.USER_CD = KOK.USER_CD     LEFT JOIN HN2MAS HN2 ON TAI.KURACD = HN2.CLI_CD                           AND TAI.ACBCD = HN2.HAN_CD     LEFT JOIN HAIMAS HAI ON SUBSTR(HN2.CLI_CD,2,2) = HAI.KEN_CD                           AND HN2.HAISO_CD = HAI.HAISO_CD     LEFT JOIN M06_PULLDOWN PL6 ON PL6.KBN = '03' AND PL6.CD = TAI.SHUGOU     LEFT JOIN TEL ON TAI.SYONO = TEL.SEQNO  WHERE  1 = 1  AND TAI.KURACD >= :KURACD_FROM  AND TAI.KURACD <= :KURACD_TO  AND TAI.SYOYMD BETWEEN :TRGDATE_FROM AND :TRGDATE_TO  AND (TAI.HATKBN = :HATKBN1 OR TAI.HATKBN = :HATKBN2)  AND (TAI.TAIOKBN = :TAIOKBN1 OR TAI.TAIOKBN = :TAIOKBN2)  ORDER BY     KURACD,     ACBCD,     HATYMD,     HATTIME
